  Register Map

Chapter 09      
A0~AF       
B0~BF       
C0~CF       
D0~DF       
E0~EF       
 
 
Note: 
1. Address marked with 
   is not existed in 5725. 
2. All registers (except chapter 01  status register is read only) have default value “0x00” after power up. 
3. All registers require segment for access. Segment is defined in address F0. 
For example: 
          S1_46 means F0 must be set to 1 before accessing 46  
                       S1_46=8D equal following operation: 
    F 0  =  0 1  
    4 6  =  8 D   
 
 Address Segment

 RD-5725-1.1  01—1
  Chapter   01 ． INPUT FORMATTER REGISTERS  
 
INPUT_FORMATTER 00 REG S1_00, R/W 
 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0 
Bit IF_HS_FLIP IF_PRGRSV_C
NTRL IF_VS_SEL  IF_SEL16BIT IF_SEL_656 IF_UV_REVER
T IF_MATRIX_BYP
S IF_IN_DRE
G_BYPS 
 
Bit Name Function 
Input pipe by pass 
0 IF_IN_DREG_BYPS Use the falling or rising edge of clock to get the input data. 
0: Clock input data on the falling edge of ICLK. 1: Clock input date on the rising edge of ICLK. 
Rgb2yuv matrix bypass 
 1 IF_MATRIX_BYPS If source is yuv24bit, bypass the rgb2yuv matrix. 
0:source is 24bit RGB. Do rgb2yuv.  
1: data bypass. 
8bit to 16bit convert Y/UV flip control 
2 IF_UV_REVERT If input is 8bit data, when it convert to 16bit, this bit control Y and UV order: 
0: Keep the designed order 
1: Flip the Y and UV order 
Select CCIR656 data 
3 IF_SEL_656 If input data is 8bit CCIR656 mode, choose the 656 data path. 
0: input is CCIR 601 mode. Choose the CCIR601mode timing. 
1: input is CCIR 656 mode. Choose the CCIR656 mode timing. 
Select 16bit data 
4 
 IF_SEL16BIT If source data is 16bit. Choose the 16bits data path. 
Use in conjunction with register sel_24bit to choose the input data format. 
 Sel_16bit Sel_24bit 
8bit 656/601 input 0 0 
16bit 601 input 1 0 
24bit yuv/rgb 601 input * 1  
Vertical sync select 
5 IF_VS_SEL Choose the periodical or virtual vertical timing. 
0: choose the VCR mode timing generation. 
1: choose the normal mode timing generation. 
Select progressive data 
6 IF_PRGRSV_CNTRL Progressive mode. Choose the progressive data. 
0: source is interlaced. 
1: source is progressive. 
Horizontal sync flip control 
7 IF_HS_FLIP Control the horizontal sync output from CCIR process 
0: keep the original horizontal sync.  
1: flip horizontal sync.

Bit Name Function 
Vertical sync flip control 
0 IF_VS_FLIP Control the vertical sync output from CCIR process 
0: keep original vertical sync. 
1: flip vertical sync. 
YUV 422to444 UV flip control 
 1 IF_UV_FLIP Control the U and V order in yuv422to444 conversion. 
0: keep original U and V order.  1: exchange the U and V order. 
U data select in YUV 422to444 conversion 
2 IF_U_DELAY Select original U data or 1-clock delayed U data, so that it can align with V data. 
0: select original U data after dmux. 
1: select 1-clock delayed U data after dmux. 
V data select in YUV 422to444 conversion 
3 IF_V_DELAY Select original V data or 1-clock delayed V data, so that it can align with U data. 
0: select original V data after dmux. 
1: select 1-clock delayed V data after dmux. 
Tap6 interpolator bypass control in YUV 422to444 conversion 
4 
 IF_TAP6_BYPS Select the data if pass the tap6 interpolator or not. 
0: the data will pass the tap6 interpolator. 1: the data will not pass the tap6 interpolator 
Y data pipes control in YUV422to444 conversion 
6-5 IF_Y_DELAY Control the Y data pipe delay, so that it can align with U and V. 
IF_Y_DELAY Y data delay pipes 
00 1 
01 2 
10 3 
11 4

HD_BYPS 00 REG S1_30, R/W 
 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0 
Bit RESERVED HD_SEL_BLK
_IN HD_DYN_BYPS HD_MATRIX_B
YPS HD_IN_DRE
G_BYPS 
 
Bit Name Function 
Input retiming bypass 
0 HD_IN_DREG_BYPS Use the falling or rising edge of clock to get the input data. 
0: Clock input data on the falling edge 
1: Clock input date on the rising edge 
YUV2RGB conversion bypass control 
1 HD_MATRIX_BYPS Available only when input source is YUV source 
0: YUV2RGB convert 1: bypass YUV2RGB function 
Dynamic range bypass control 
2 HD_DYN_BYPS If the input is YUV data, it must do dynamic range. 
0: input is YUV data, do dynamic range . 1: input is RGB data, bypass dynamic range 
Blank select 
3 HD_SEL_BLK_IN Choose the input blank or generated blank use sync. 
0: choose the blank that sync generated. 1: choose the input blank, if the input is DVI data.

 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0 
Bit RESERVED PLL_MS PLL_ADS PLL_IS PLL_DIVBY2Z PLL_CKIS 
 
Bit Name Function 
CKIS, PLL source clock selection 
0 PLL_CKIS When = 0, PLL use OSC clock 
When = 1, PLL use input clock 
DIVBY2Z, PLL source clock divide bypass 
1 PLL_DIVBY2Z When = 0, PLL source clock divide by two 
When = 1, PLL source clock bypass divide 
IS, ICLK source selection 
2 PLL_IS When = 0, ICLK  use PLL clock 
When = 1, ICLK use input clock  
ADS, input clock selection 
3 PLL_ADS When = 0, input clock is from PCLKIN(pin40) 
When = 1, input clock is from ADC 
MS[2:0], memory clock control 
6-4 PLL_MS When = 000, memory clock =108MHz 
When = 001, memory clock = 81MHz 
When = 010, memory clock from FBCLK (pin110) 
When = 011, memory clock = 162MHz When = 100, memory clock = 144MHz When = 101, memory clock = 185MHz 
When = 110, memory clock = 216MHz 
When = 111, memory clock = 129.6Mhz 
Reserved 7 RESERVED

MEMORY CONTROLLER 00  REG S4_00, R/W 
 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0 
Bit MEM_INI_REG 
 
Bit Name Function 
SDRAM Idle Period Control and IDLE Done Select : (default 0)  
1-0 MEM_INI_REG [1:0] MEM_INI_REG [1:0] #of VS (vertical syn) 
0 0 2 
0 1 3 
1 0 1 
1 1 R_MSOFTH  
Software Control SDRAM Idle Period: 
2 MEM_INI_REG [2] When this bit is 1, software programming will control the idle period to access 
memory.this bit is useful only when th e register r_mslidl[1:0] sets 2’b11. 
Reserved  3 MEM_INI_REG [3]  
SDRAM Reset Signal:  
4 MEM_INI_REG [4] When this bit is 1, will generate 5-mmclk pulse, and reset memory controller 
timing, data pipe and state machine; 
Reserved 5 MEM_INI_REG [5]  
Initial Cycle Mode Select: 
6 MEM_INI_REG [6] When this bit is 1, then during initia l period, the mode cycle will go before 
refresh cycle; otherwise refresh cycle will be before mode cycle. 
SDRAM Start Initial Cycle: 
7 MEM_INI_REG [7] This register should work with the register 80/[2:0] ; 
When this bit is 1, memory controller initial cycle enable; 
When this bit is 0, memory co ntroller initial cycle disable.

  MEMORY CONTROLLER 16 REG S4_10, R/W 
 7 6 5 4 3 2 1 0 
Bit RESERVED MEM_MISC_REG 
 
Bit Name FUNCTION 
Control Write Enable (DQM) High Bits 
0 MEM_MISC_REG [0] Don’t care, default value 0,  In 5705 chip, this register will not be on effect, it use 
for future. 
Control Active State before Refresh Cycle  
1 MEM_MISC_REG [1]  Don’t care, default value 1, This register  will on effect when set “8D/7” is 1.  
When this bit sets 1 ,will generate a signal to pull down the act cycle done signal 
after refresh cycle ,make it be one mmclk pulse ;or will make this signal be level 
. 
SDRAM SAFE REAE/WRITE OPERATION 
2 MEM_MISC_REG [2] Don’t care, default value 0, 
When this bit sets 1, will make state machine calculate up during read/write operation. When this bit sets 0, will make state machine hold during read/write operation 
Add No Operation For Precharge Cycle 
3 MEM_MISC_REG [3] Don’t care, default value 0;  
When this bit sets 0, will add NOP for precharge cycle ; 
When this bit sets 1,will no add NOP for precharge cycle. 
Turn Off Qualified Active Cycle Done: default value 0;  
4 MEM_MISC_REG [4] This register is 1, will shut off active state after refresh cycle. 
This register is 0, will turn on active state after refresh cycle; 
RESERVED 7-5 RESERVED

Bit Name Function 
External sync enable, active high 
0 VDS_SYNC_EN This bit enable sync lock mode. 
vds_flock_en (1A[4]) vds_sync_en VDS timing 
0 0 Free run 
0 1 Sync lock 
1 X Frame lock  
ABAB double field mode enable 
1 VDS_FIELDAB_EN In field double mode, when this bit is 1,  VDS works in ABAB mode, otherwise it 
works in AABB mode.  
Double field mode enable active high 
2 VDS_DFIELD_EN This bit enable field double mode, ex, fr ame rate from 50Hz to 100Hz, or from 
60Hz to 120Hz. When this bit is 1, the output timing is interlaced.  
Flip field control. 
3 VDS_FIELD_FLIP This bit is field flip control bit, it only  used in interlace mode. When it is 1, it 
inverts the output field.  
Horizontal scale up bypass control,  active high 4 VDS_HSCALE_BYPS When this bit is 1, data will bypass horizontal scale up process. 
Vertical scale up bypass control,  active high 5 VDS_VSCALE_BYPS When this bit is 1, data will by pass vertical scale up process. 
Horizontal scale up bypass control,  active high 6 VDS_HALF_EN  
Horizontal scale up bypass control,  active high 7 VDS_SRESET When this bit is 1, it reset the VDS_PROC internal module ds_video_enhance,

more frames.
